# StoryForge — Build Plan

> **Source of truth for what we're building, in what order, and what's done.**
> Update this file as we go. Ship one task at a time.

## Status legend

- `[ ]` pending
- `[~]` in progress
- `[x]` done
- `[!]` blocked
- `[-]` dropped / deprioritized

Effort tags: `S` (≤2h), `M` (half-day), `L` (1–2 days), `XL` (3+ days)

---

## Decisions made

- **Build mode**: SaaS (Option C)
- **Auth**: Clerk
- **DB**: SQLite (Phase 2) → Neon Postgres (Phase 3)
- **ORM**: SQLModel
- **File storage**: Cloudflare R2 in Phase 3 (local disk in Phase 2)
- **Frontend host**: Vercel
- **Backend host**: Render
- **Payments**: Stripe (scaffold in M3, enable later)
- **Default Claude model**: `claude-sonnet-4-6` (override via `STORYFORGE_MODEL`)

## Decisions pending (answer before M3)

- [ ] **D1**: Target user — PMs / BAs / Eng managers / Founders? (Drives templates + integrations.)
- [ ] **D2**: Wedge — what makes us non-commodity? (Custom templates? Source citations? Multi-doc? Workflow?)
- [ ] **D3**: BYOK or managed Anthropic key? (Drives billing model.)
- [ ] **D4**: Free-tier limits — runs/month? doc size cap? feature gates?
- [ ] **D5**: Pricing — per-seat vs per-run vs per-doc?

---

# M0 — Operations (cross-cutting)

> Start in M2. Don't wait until the end.

## M0.1 Testing

- [x] **M0.1.1** Add `pytest` to backend, write smoke test for `/api/extract` mock path — `backend/tests/` — S _(26 tests across `test_isolation.py` (9), `test_limits.py` (6), `test_billing.py` (11). Shared `conftest.py` pins throwaway SQLite + dummy keys before importing main, stubs Clerk/Resend, and exposes `client` + `as_user` fixtures via dependency_overrides on `current_user`. Per-test cleanup wipes test-user rows so ownership-counting assertions stay deterministic. All green in 1.8s.)_
- [x] **M0.1.2** Vitest + React Testing Library + jsdom scaffold; first smoke test on `EditableText` (foundation of M4.1 inline editing) — `frontend/vite.config.js`, `frontend/src/test/` — S
- [~] **M0.1.3** Playwright installed + 2 smoke specs against public unauth surfaces (sign-in renders, /share/<bogus-token> shows not-found). Full upload→extract happy path deferred to M0.1.3.b — needs `STORYFORGE_E2E_USER_ID` Clerk auth-bypass dep override on backend — `frontend/playwright.config.js`, `frontend/e2e/`, `.github/workflows/ci.yml` — M
- [~] **M0.1.4** Coverage measured + reported in CI (54% baseline at first run); `--cov-fail-under` threshold deferred until we add tests for streaming + regen + comments paths — `backend/requirements.txt`, `.github/workflows/ci.yml` — S

## M0.2 CI/CD

- [x] **M0.2.1** GitHub Actions: backend test + lint on PR — `.github/workflows/ci.yml` — S _(merged with M0.2.2 into a single `ci.yml` with `backend` + `frontend` jobs. Backend job runs `pytest -v` on Python 3.13 with pip caching keyed off `requirements.txt`. Triggers on push to main + all PRs.)_
- [x] **M0.2.2** GitHub Actions: frontend test + build on PR — `.github/workflows/ci.yml` — S _(see M0.2.1 — single workflow file. Frontend job runs `npm run build` on Node 20 with npm cache + a `pk_test_ci_placeholder_key` so Vite doesn't crash on the required `VITE_CLERK_PUBLISHABLE_KEY` import-time env check.)_
- [ ] **M0.2.3** Auto-deploy to Render (backend) + Vercel (frontend) on `main` — — S
- [ ] **M0.2.4** Block merge if tests fail — repo settings — S

## M0.3 Observability

- [x] **M0.3.1** Structured logging in FastAPI (JSON logs) — `backend/services/obs.py` — S _(see M0.3.2 — same module.)_
- [x] **M0.3.2** Request ID middleware — `backend/services/obs.py` — S _(new [services/obs.py](backend/services/obs.py): `JsonFormatter` emits one-line JSON per record (ts/level/logger/msg + rid + exc), `RequestIdMiddleware` mints `uuid4().hex[:12]` (or trusts inbound `X-Request-Id`), binds it to a `ContextVar` so logs auto-attach it, echoes `X-Request-Id` back in the response, and emits one access log per request with `method path -> status in Xms`. Wired before CORS in main.py so OPTIONS preflights also get an id.)_
- [x] **M0.3.3** Anthropic token usage emitted as a structured log line per Claude call (action, model, in/out/cache tokens, cost_usd, extraction_id) — joins JSON pipeline alongside access logs — `backend/services/extractions.py` — S
- [x] **M0.3.4** Sentry (frontend + backend) — — S _(backend half: [services/obs.py](backend/services/obs.py) `install_sentry()` silent no-op without `SENTRY_DSN`. Frontend half (M0 polish run): [lib/sentry.js](frontend/src/lib/sentry.js) `initSentry()` mirrors backend pattern — silent no-op without `VITE_SENTRY_DSN`; called from main.jsx before mount so import-time crashes are captured; `setSentryUser()` tags events with Clerk user_id + org_id, called from App.jsx via useUser. No PII (just ids). Trace sampling default 0; opt in via `VITE_SENTRY_TRACES_RATE`. Both keys + ENV variants wired in render.yaml + Dockerfile build args.)_
- [x] **M0.3.5** PostHog analytics — code-split SDK (62 KB on-demand chunk, 0 KB when key unset); 7-event taxonomy (extraction_started/finished/failed, export_clicked, share_link_created, regen_clicked, comment_posted); user identified by Clerk id + org tag, no PII — `frontend/src/lib/analytics.js` — M

## M0.4 Documentation

- [x] **M0.4.1** `README.md` at root — quickstart, dev loop, env vars — — S
- [x] **M0.4.2** `CONTRIBUTING.md` — branch model, commit style, PR template, where-to-make-changes table — — S
- [x] **M0.4.3** `.gitignore` audit — added coverage outputs, Playwright caches, `*.egg-info`, `frontend/coverage/`, `.eslintcache` — — S
- [x] **M0.4.4** Mermaid architecture diagram in README, replaces stale ASCII art; updated stack details to reflect M3+M4+M5 reality (Postgres / R2 / LSQ / Resend / Sentry / Vitest / dnd-kit) — — S

# M1 — Foundations / UI honesty (Phase 1)

> Goal: stop showing controls that lie. Make every visible thing work, even if minimally.
> Frontend-only, localStorage backed. ~3–5 days.

## M1.1 Slim the sidebar

- [x] **M1.1.1** Remove decorative sidebar items: Chats, Templates, Projects section, Recent uploads, free-trial progress bar, account-picker dropdown affordance — `frontend/src/components/Sidebar.jsx` — S
- [x] **M1.1.2** Keep: logo, app name, search icon (stub w/ tooltip "Coming soon"), `+ New` icon (resets to upload screen), Documents nav, Settings nav, user pill — `Sidebar.jsx` — S
- [x] **M1.1.3** Add active state when route is `/documents` or `/settings` (lift the active prop from App) — `Sidebar.jsx`, `App.jsx` — S _(rolled into M1.2.2; NavLink derives active state from route, `active` prop dropped entirely)_
- [ ] **M1.1.4** User pill click opens a small popover with "Sign out" (no-op for now), "Settings" link — `Sidebar.jsx` — S

## M1.2 Routing (lightweight)

- [x] **M1.2.1** Add `react-router-dom@6` and wire 3 routes: `/` (home/extract), `/documents`, `/settings` — `frontend/package.json`, `App.jsx`, `main.jsx` — S _(landed v7.14.2 — same API surface)_
- [x] **M1.2.2** Sidebar nav items become `<NavLink>`s — `Sidebar.jsx` — S
- [x] **M1.2.3** `/` redirects to last extraction if one is loaded, else shows EmptyState — `App.jsx` — S _(behavior already implicit in the `/` route's conditional render; added defensive `navigate('/')` on extraction success so a future trigger from `/documents` lands the user on the result)_

## M1.3 Documents view (localStorage MVP)

- [x] **M1.3.1** On extraction success, persist `{id, filename, savedAt, payload}` to `localStorage['storyforge:extractions']` (cap at 50) — `App.jsx` or new `frontend/src/lib/store.js` — M
- [x] **M1.3.2** Build `frontend/src/pages/Documents.jsx` — list view: filename, savedAt, story count, gaps count — M
- [x] **M1.3.3** Click row → restore extraction into App state, navigate to `/` — — S
- [x] **M1.3.4** Row hover: show delete icon; click confirms via toast (undo for 5s) — — M
- [x] **M1.3.5** Empty state on Documents page (no uploads yet) with CTA back to `/` — — S _(shipped as part of M1.3.2 — `<EmptyState>` component inside Documents.jsx with "No documents yet" + primary "New extraction" button)_
- [x] **M1.3.6** Search box filters by filename or any text in the brief — — S _(also matches against brief tags)_

## M1.4 Settings page

- [x] **M1.4.1** Build `frontend/src/pages/Settings.jsx` — three sections: API, Model, Appearance — M
- [x] **M1.4.2** API section: text field for `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` (BYOK mode), masked, "Test connection" button hits `/api/health` — M _(button hits new `/api/test-key` for an actual auth round-trip rather than just `/api/health` which only checks env presence; also added show/hide toggle, status dot, and Remove action)_
- [x] **M1.4.3** Backend: accept BYOK via `X-Anthropic-Key` header on `/api/extract`, override env key per request — `backend/main.py`, `backend/extract.py` — M
- [x] **M1.4.4** Model section: radio group with Opus 4.7 / Sonnet 4.6 / Haiku 4.5 — pricing shown per option — S _(card-style radio with 4 options including "Server default"; per-request override via new `X-Storyforge-Model` header)_
- [x] **M1.4.5** Appearance section: theme radio (light/dark/system) — S _(card-row picker w/ Sun/Moon/Monitor icons; system mode follows `prefers-color-scheme` and reacts to OS-level theme changes via mediaQuery listener)_
- [x] **M1.4.6** Persist all settings to `localStorage['storyforge:settings']` and read on app boot — `frontend/src/lib/settings.js` — S _(persistence layer existed since M1.4.2; M1.4.5 wired the boot-read for theme. API key + model already read on each request via `authHeaders()`)_

## M1.5 Active tab pills (artifacts pane)

- [x] **M1.5.1** Tab pills become buttons that scroll the corresponding section into view (smooth) — `ArtifactsPane.jsx` — S _(also dropped the misleading "Gaps" tab — gaps live in the rail, not the pane)_
- [x] **M1.5.2** Active tab highlights as user scrolls (IntersectionObserver) — `ArtifactsPane.jsx` — M _(IO with `rootMargin: '-30% 0px -65% 0px'` — 5% trigger band 30% from the top; tab pills are sticky to top so they stay visible while scrolling)_

## M1.6 Gap actions (resolve / ignore / ask)

- [x] **M1.6.1** Per-gap state in localStorage keyed by extraction id + gap index: `{resolved: bool, ignored: bool, askedAt: ts}` — `lib/store.js` — S
- [x] **M1.6.2** Resolved gap: strikethrough + green check, count in header subtracts — `GapsRail.jsx` — S _(also resolved gaps sink to bottom of active list, dimmed; "Reopen" link to undo)_
- [x] **M1.6.3** Ignored gap: collapses into a "3 ignored" footer that expands on click — `GapsRail.jsx` — M _(footer is a dashed-border button; expanded list shows compact rows with Restore link)_
- [x] **M1.6.4** Ask stakeholder: copies a formatted markdown question to clipboard, shows toast — `GapsRail.jsx` — S _(markdown includes Question/Severity/Source/Context; sets askedAt + shows "Asked" badge; copy fallback for legacy browsers via execCommand)_

## M1.7 Toasts + tooltips

- [x] **M1.7.1** Build `frontend/src/components/Toast.jsx` (provider + `useToast()` hook) — M
- [x] **M1.7.2** Replace all inline error spans with `toast.error(...)` — sweep of all components — S
- [x] **M1.7.3** Add `title` attr to every IconButton for tooltips (free, native) — sweep — S _(IconButton primitive already wires `title={label}` + `aria-label={label}` from M1.7.1; sweep found one raw `<button>` (file-chip × in EmptyState) missing — added)_

## M1.8 Mobile responsive

- [-] **M1.8.1** Below 1024px: sidebar collapses behind a hamburger; off-canvas overlay — `Sidebar.jsx`, `App.jsx` — L _(deferred 2026-04-23 — desktop-first for v1; revisit when mobile users become a target)_
- [-] **M1.8.2** Below 768px: source pane and artifacts pane stack vertically with a tab switch — `App.jsx` — L _(deferred 2026-04-23 — same)_
- [-] **M1.8.3** Gaps rail becomes a bottom-sheet on mobile — `GapsRail.jsx` — M _(deferred 2026-04-23 — same)_

## M1.9 Polish

- [x] **M1.9.1** Empty state inside ArtifactsPane when one section returns 0 items — already partial; sweep — S _(verified: Actors / Stories / NFRs all use `<EmptySection>`; Brief is schema-required so always renders)_
- [x] **M1.9.2** Sort gaps by severity already done — verify and add a "filter by severity" pill row — S _(All / High / Medium / Low pill row with per-bucket counts; pill disabled at count 0; appears only when more than 1 active gap exists)_
- [x] **M1.9.3** Copy-per-artifact: hover any story/gap reveals a copy icon — `ArtifactsPane.jsx`, `GapsRail.jsx` — M _(generic `.has-action`/`.row-action` CSS class; copy buttons emit markdown via shared `lib/clipboard.js`; story copy includes ID/actor/want/so-that/section/criteria; gap copy uses the same markdown as Ask but doesn't set askedAt)_

**M1 ship gate**: all sidebar items either work or are removed. Documents page lists past extractions. Settings persists API key + model. No fake controls.

**M1 status (2026-04-23):** ✅ **Shipped (27/30)** — all 8 active sub-modules complete. M1.8 (mobile responsive, 3 tasks) deferred per user decision; revisit when mobile users become a target.

# M2 — Persistence (Phase 2)

> Goal: your work survives a refresh and is the seed of a real backend data model.
> SQLite. Single file. Zero infra cost. ~1–2 weeks.

## M2.1 SQLite + SQLModel schema

- [x] **M2.1.1** Add `sqlmodel`, `aiosqlite` to `backend/requirements.txt`; install — S _(installed `sqlmodel 0.0.38`; skipped `aiosqlite` — using sync sessions on FastAPI's threadpool, simpler for our load. Trivial to add later if we go async)_
- [x] **M2.1.2** Define schema in `backend/db/models.py`: `Extraction(id, filename, raw_text, brief_json, actors_json, stories_json, nfrs_json, gaps_json, created_at, model_used, project_id?, source_file_path?)` — M
- [x] **M2.1.3** Define `Project(id, name, created_at)` and `GapState(id, extraction_id, gap_idx, resolved, ignored, asked_at)` — S _(GapState uses composite PK on `(extraction_id, gap_idx)` — gaps have no stable id from the model)_
- [x] **M2.1.4** SQLite engine + session dependency in `backend/db/session.py` — S
- [x] **M2.1.5** Auto-create tables on startup (FastAPI lifespan event) — `main.py` — S
- [-] **M2.1.6** Add `alembic` for future migrations — `backend/alembic/` — M _(deferred 2026-04-23 — `SQLModel.metadata.create_all()` is sufficient until our first schema change in production. Real need is the Postgres migration at M3.2 — set up alembic then)_

## M2.2 Backend CRUD routes

- [x] **M2.2.1** `POST /api/extract` writes to DB, returns `Extraction` with `id` — `main.py`, `extract.py` — S
- [x] **M2.2.2** `GET /api/extractions` paginated list — `backend/routers/extractions.py` — M _(supports `q`, `project_id`, `limit`, `offset`; returns `ExtractionSummary` rows — no `raw_text`/payload to keep the list lean)_
- [x] **M2.2.3** `GET /api/extractions/{id}` — — S
- [x] **M2.2.4** `DELETE /api/extractions/{id}` — — S _(cascades gap states manually since the schema has no SA cascade)_
- [x] **M2.2.5** `PATCH /api/extractions/{id}` (rename, move to project) — — S _(empty `project_id` clears the link; non-empty validated against existing project)_
- [x] **M2.2.6** `PATCH /api/extractions/{id}/gaps/{idx}` — resolve/ignore — — S _(upserts the GapState row; bounds-checked against `extraction.gaps`)_
- [x] **M2.2.7** Project routes: `GET / POST /api/projects`, `DELETE /api/projects/{id}`, `PATCH /api/projects/{id}` — M _(delete detaches extractions rather than cascading — losing a project shouldn't lose work)_

## M2.3 Source-file storage

- [x] **M2.3.1** Save uploaded file to `backend/uploads/{extraction_id}/{filename}` — `main.py` — S _(extraction id minted up front so the path is known before the row exists; disk write happens before persist so a save failure 500s without leaving an orphan row)_
- [x] **M2.3.2** `GET /api/extractions/{id}/source` returns the original file with correct mimetype — — S _(mimetypes.guess_type with `.md`/`.markdown`/`.rst` registered explicitly; 404 for missing row, paste-mode extraction, or vanished file — same user-facing answer)_
- [x] **M2.3.3** Cleanup hook on delete — — S _(`delete_extraction` calls `remove_upload_dir` after the row is gone — best-effort, non-blocking)_

## M2.4 Frontend Documents view (server-backed)

- [x] **M2.4.1** Replace localStorage reads with calls to `/api/extractions` — `Documents.jsx` — S
- [-] **M2.4.2** Add `react-query` (TanStack Query) for caching + refetch — `frontend/package.json` — M _(deferred 2026-04-24 — plain `useEffect` + a refresh helper covers the current surface area: a single list view, a detail fetch on open, and per-gap optimistic patches. Add react-query when we hit M2.5/M2.6 and need cross-page cache invalidation)_
- [x] **M2.4.3** Loading + error skeletons on Documents page — — S
- [x] **M2.4.4** Restore extraction → fetches `/api/extractions/{id}` → hydrates App state — — S _(App.restoreExtraction now branches: full record opens immediately; summary row triggers `getExtraction(id)` and toasts on 404)_
- [x] **M2.4.5** Migration helper: on first load, push localStorage extractions to backend, clear localStorage — `lib/migrate.js` — M _(idempotent — preserves original ids; sticky `storyforge:migrated:v1` flag prevents reruns; only clears local on full success)_

## M2.5 Projects (group extractions)

- [x] **M2.5.1** Re-add the Projects section in Sidebar (this time backed by API) — `Sidebar.jsx` — S _(`AppContext` now caches `{projects, projectsLoading, refreshProjects, projectById}` so the sidebar, Documents pill, and Project page all share one source of truth)_
- [x] **M2.5.2** "+ New project" inline form in sidebar — — S _(small +/× toggle on the section header; Enter submits, Esc/× cancel; auto-focuses input on open)_
- [x] **M2.5.3** Project page: `frontend/src/pages/Project.jsx` — list of extractions in this project — M _(inline-rename header, ghost Delete project button with confirm prompt — delete *detaches* extractions per backend, doesn't cascade; per-row "Remove from project" + Delete actions; reuses the Documents row layout)_
- [x] **M2.5.4** Move-to-project from Documents row context menu — — S _(MoreHorizontal "…" button per row → popover with project list + "Remove from project" footer; click-outside catcher + Esc to close; row also gets an accent-pill linking to the parent project)_

## M2.6 Versioning

- [x] **M2.6.1** "Re-run on this doc" button on an extraction → creates a new version, links to parent — `ArtifactsPane.jsx`, backend — M _(landed in TopBar instead of ArtifactsPane — better with the existing breadcrumb context. New `POST /api/extractions/{id}/rerun` reuses the saved `raw_text`+`filename` and applies the current request's API key + model so users can re-run with a different model)_
- [x] **M2.6.2** Version dropdown in TopBar shows v1, v2, v3 — — M _(badge "v{N} of {total}" only renders when total > 1; click opens a popover with each version's id, timestamp, model, and a Check next to current; click any to switch — the studio re-hydrates from the backend so no stale state carries over)_
- [!] **M2.6.3** Diff view (later) — `[!]` deferred to M5 — —

## M2.7 Search

- [x] **M2.7.1** Backend: `GET /api/extractions?q=foo` — substring across filename + brief — S _(case-insensitive substring on filename + `json_extract(brief, '$.summary')` via `func.json_extract`; tag search left out — JSON-array LIKE in SQLite is fiddly, revisit if usage shows demand)_
- [x] **M2.7.2** Frontend: search box on Documents wired to query — — S _(replaced the client-side useMemo filter with a 200 ms debounced effect that re-queries `/api/extractions?q=...`; inline Spinner next to the count badge while a search is in flight; "no docs yet" hero only shows when the store is genuinely empty, not when a search returns 0)_

**M2 ship gate**: Refresh keeps your work. Multiple extractions visible in a real Documents page. Projects exist. Source files retrievable.

---

# M3 — Auth + SaaS foundation (Phase 3)

> Goal: real users, isolated data, billing scaffolding.
> Clerk + Neon Postgres + Stripe scaffold + R2 storage. ~2–3 weeks.

## M3.1 Clerk integration

- [x] **M3.1.1** Sign up at clerk.com, get publishable + secret keys — — S _(Clerk app `sweeping-fawn-26`; keys live in `backend/.env` (`CLERK_SECRET_KEY`) + `frontend/.env` (`VITE_CLERK_PUBLISHABLE_KEY`); secret verified via `GET https://api.clerk.com/v1/users` → 200)_
- [x] **M3.1.2** Frontend: `@clerk/clerk-react` — wrap App in `<ClerkProvider>` — `main.jsx` — S _(via `ClerkRouterAdapter` so Clerk uses react-router's navigate instead of full-page reloads)_
- [x] **M3.1.3** Add `<SignIn />` and `<SignUp />` pages, redirect unauth users to sign-in — M _(`pages/SignInPage.jsx` + `pages/SignUpPage.jsx` mount Clerk's hosted widgets; `<SignedIn>`/`<SignedOut>` gate at the route level — anything except `/sign-in/*` and `/sign-up/*` redirects when signed out)_
- [x] **M3.1.4** User pill in sidebar pulls from `useUser()`; sign-out button — `Sidebar.jsx` — S _(new `UserPill` reads name/email via `useUser()`; Clerk's `<UserButton>` renders a 28px avatar with the manage-account + sign-out dropdown built in, `afterSignOutUrl="/sign-in"`)_
- [x] **M3.1.5** Backend: install `clerk-sdk-python`, validate JWT on every `/api/*` request — `backend/auth/clerk.py` — M _(switched to **PyJWT + JWKS verification** — `clerk-sdk-python` adds churn risk for what's effectively 30 lines of JWT code. `_derive_issuer_from_pk` decodes the publishable key's base64-encoded host to get the JWKS URL. Issuer + algorithm checked; aud verification disabled because Clerk doesn't set it. New dep: `pyjwt[crypto]>=2.8.0`)_
- [x] **M3.1.6** FastAPI dependency `current_user` extracts user_id from JWT — `backend/auth/deps.py` — S _(returns frozen `CurrentUser(user_id, org_id, org_role)` dataclass; routes that need the user parametrise, routes that just need auth-gating use `dependencies=[Depends(current_user)]`)_
- [x] **M3.1.7** All routes require auth; reject with 401 if no/invalid token — — S _(router-level dependency on `extractions_router` and `projects_router` covers everything under `/api/extractions` and `/api/projects`; explicit `Depends(current_user)` on `/api/extract` and `/api/test-key` in main.py; `/api/health` deliberately left open for infra probes. **Note**: data is not yet user-filtered — all signed-in users see all rows. M3.2 adds the user_id column + per-query filtering)_

## M3.2 Postgres migration + isolation

- [x] **M3.2.1** Sign up at neon.tech, create project + DB — — S _(switched to **Supabase** instead — same Postgres under the hood. Connection string in gitignored `backend/.env` as `DATABASE_URL`. Free tier: 500 MB, pauses after 1 week inactivity (5s wake on first request). PostgreSQL 17.6.)_
- [x] **M3.2.2** Add `psycopg[binary]` + `asyncpg` to requirements — S _(only `psycopg[binary]>=3.1.0` — `asyncpg` not needed since SQLModel sessions are sync. Async swap is a future optimisation)_
- [x] **M3.2.3** Update `DATABASE_URL` env var, swap engine to Postgres — `backend/db/session.py` — S _(dialect-aware: `DATABASE_URL` env var picks Postgres (forces `postgresql+psycopg://` so SQLAlchemy doesn't default to legacy psycopg2); unset falls back to SQLite at `STORYFORGE_DB`. `connect_args` differ per dialect (`check_same_thread=False` for SQLite only). `pool_pre_ping=True` on Postgres so dropped connections to Supabase reconnect cleanly. Soft migrations gated to SQLite — Postgres goes through Alembic when M3.2.5 lands)_
- [x] **M3.2.4** Add `user_id` (Clerk's `user_xxx`) column to all tables — `db/models.py` — M _(landed on SQLite ahead of Postgres migration. Soft `ALTER TABLE` adds `extraction.user_id` and `project.user_id` with `DEFAULT 'local'` — existing rows backfill to "local". `usage_log.user_id` and `user_settings.user_id` already existed from M3.0. `org_id` deferred to M3.3 with workspaces)_
- [-] **M3.2.5** Generate Alembic migration for the schema change — — S _(deferred — `create_all` bootstrapped Postgres cleanly with the M3.0/3.1/3.2 schema baked in, so there's no schema *change* to migrate yet. Set up Alembic when the next column lands (likely M3.4.4 user-settings PUT route or M3.5.4 free-tier limits). Until then, Postgres tracks SQLModel's metadata directly)_
- [x] **M3.2.6** Every query filters by `current_user.user_id` (or `org_id` if Workspaces enabled) — sweep all routers — M _(every route in `routers/extractions.py` + `routers/projects.py` + `/api/extract` + `/api/extractions/import` now filters by `current_user.user_id`. Cross-user reads return **404 not 403** to avoid existence leaks. Project ownership validated before LLM call so we don't waste tokens. New `_owned_extraction()` + `_owned_project()` helpers centralise the check)_
- [x] **M3.2.7** Test: User A cannot see User B's extractions — `tests/test_isolation.py` — M _(22-assertion script; uses TestClient + `dependency_overrides` on `current_user` so no real Clerk JWT needed. Throwaway DB via `STORYFORGE_DB` env var. Runs as `python -m tests.test_isolation`. All checks pass — A's project + extraction invisible to B in list / detail / versions / gaps / source; B can't PATCH/DELETE/rerun A's rows; B can't attach new extraction to A's project; B's import to A's id returns 409 collision)_

## M3.3 Workspaces / orgs

- [x] **M3.3.1** Enable Clerk Organizations in dashboard — — S _(verified live via `GET https://api.clerk.com/v1/organizations` → 200)_
- [x] **M3.3.2** Add org switcher in Sidebar (Clerk's `<OrganizationSwitcher />`) — S _(rendered above the nav, full-width with custom appearance to match the sidebar style; `hidePersonal=false` so users keep "Personal account" as a switchable context — matches our backend personal-vs-org scope rule)_
- [x] **M3.3.3** Backend: scope all queries to `org_id` if user is in an org context — M _(new `services/scope.py` with `apply_scope(stmt, model, user)` and `in_scope(row, user)`. Personal context: `WHERE user_id=:uid AND org_id IS NULL`. Org context: `WHERE org_id=:org_id` (every member sees every org row — workspace = shared). Schema: `org_id` columns added to extraction/project/usage_log via dialect-aware `_apply_soft_migrations` (now uses `inspect(engine)` so it works on both SQLite and Postgres). Routes refactored: `_owned_extraction` + `_owned_project` use `in_scope`; list/usage/export queries use `apply_scope`; persist/record_usage take `org_id`. `/api/me/legacy` adoption stays personal-only by design — orphan dev rows go into the user's personal scope, not whichever org happens to be active)_
- [x] **M3.3.4** Invite teammate flow (Clerk handles UI) — S _(invitation/management UI lives inside Clerk's `<OrganizationSwitcher>` dropdown — no extra code needed)_

## M3.4 BYOK encrypted at rest

- [x] **M3.4.1** Generate a `MASTER_KEY` env var for the backend — — S _(M3.0 — `STORYFORGE_MASTER_KEY` env var; dev fallback generates an ephemeral key + warns)_
- [x] **M3.4.2** Encrypt user's Anthropic key with Fernet (cryptography lib) before DB write — `backend/services/byok.py` — M _(M3.0 — `encrypt_secret`/`decrypt_secret`, lru-cached cipher, InvalidToken returns None for graceful key-rotation handling)_
- [x] **M3.4.3** UserSettings table: `(user_id, anthropic_key_encrypted, model_default)` — `db/models.py` — S _(M3.0 — schema only, default `user_id="local"`. Routes land with M3.4.4)_
- [x] **M3.4.4** Settings page calls `PUT /api/me/settings` instead of localStorage — `Settings.jsx` — S _(new `routers/me.py` with `GET /api/me/settings` (returns `{anthropic_key_set, anthropic_key_preview, model_default, updated_at}` — never raw key) and `PUT /api/me/settings` (Fernet-encrypted before write). [Settings.jsx](frontend/src/pages/Settings.jsx) ApiKeyForm + ModelPicker now read/write via the API; raw key only lives in component state during edit, dropped on Save. [lib/settings.js](frontend/src/lib/settings.js) shrunk to theme-only with back-compat shims. Status pill shows ••••XYZK preview)_
- [x] **M3.4.5** Extract route decrypts user's key per request, never logs it — `extract.py` — S _(new `services/byok.resolve_user_byok(session, user_id, header_override)` returns `(api_key, model)` with precedence: request header > stored UserSettings > env. Wired into `/api/extract` (main.py) and `/api/extractions/{id}/rerun`. The header path is preserved so `Test connection` keeps working without saving. Frontend [api.js](frontend/src/api.js) no longer sends `X-Anthropic-Key`/`X-Storyforge-Model` on regular requests — only `testApiKey` sends header for one-shot validation)_
- [x] **M3.4.6** Managed-key path behind `STORYFORGE_BYOK_MODE` env var. Three modes: `strict` (default — user must BYOK; server env never used for live extraction), `managed` (server pays; user keys ignored, UI hides BYOK form), `choice` (user can BYOK or fall back to server env). `services/byok.byok_mode()` + mode-aware `resolve_user_byok` in [services/byok.py](backend/services/byok.py); [extract.py](backend/extract.py) drops its own env fallback so the resolver is authoritative; `byok_mode` field on `UserSettingsRead` ([models.py](backend/models.py)) so [Settings.jsx](frontend/src/pages/Settings.jsx) renders the right copy/UI per mode. [.env.example](backend/.env.example) documents all three values — M

## M3.5 Free-tier limits

- [x] **M3.5.4** Free tier: 10 extractions / month, 25 KB doc cap. Enforce server-side — `routers/extractions.py` — M _(numbers superseded by DECISIONS.md — Trial 10 ext + 200k char cap, Starter 25 + 200k chars, Pro 100 + 400k chars, Team 300 + 800k chars. New `services/plans.py` (PLANS dict — single source of truth), `services/limits.py` `enforce_limits()` runs in `/api/extract` + `/rerun` before the Claude call. Four gates: trial expiry → 403, model not allowed → 403, doc too large → 413, monthly cap → 429. All raise structured `{paywall: true, reason, current_plan, upgrade_to, message, ...extras}`)_
- [x] **M3.5.5** Frontend: real "X of 10 runs used" bar in sidebar — `Sidebar.jsx` — S _(new `UsageBar` between nav + UserPill; reads `plan` from AppContext (App.jsx fetches `/api/me/plan` on mount + after each extract/rerun); tier-toned badge + monospace count + thin progress bar that turns warn at 80% / danger at 100%; click → `/account`)_
- [x] **M3.5.6** Hit limit → show paywall modal — M _(new [components/PaywallModal.jsx](frontend/src/components/PaywallModal.jsx) — scrim + dialog with reason-specific icon/title, "Upgrade to {tier}" CTA navigating to /account, Esc + click-outside dismisses. Triggered from App.jsx `handleExtract`/`handleRerun` catch via `e.paywall` payload)_

## M3.6 Lemon Squeezy billing (Stripe unavailable in India — see DECISIONS.md → D6)

- [x] **M3.6.1** ~~Stripe~~ **Lemon Squeezy** account, products: Starter $20 / Pro $49 / Team $99 (× monthly + annual) — S _(LSQ store `The Growth Mentor` (id 355995), USD currency, country IN. 6 published variants matching DECISIONS.md prices exactly. Test-mode credentials in `backend/.env`)_
- [x] **M3.6.2** Backend webhook handler `POST /api/webhooks/lemonsqueezy` — `routers/billing.py` — M _(HMAC-SHA256 signature verification against `LSQ_WEBHOOK_SECRET`; constant-time compare. Bad sig → 401. Missing user_id in `meta.custom_data` → 200 noop (LSQ won't retry). Raw body read before parsing so the signature matches exactly what LSQ signed)_
- [x] **M3.6.3** Plan column on User table; webhook updates plan on `customer.subscription.*` events — M _(M3.5 already added the `plan` column; M3.6 added LSQ linkage: `lsq_customer_id`, `lsq_subscription_id`, `plan_renews_at`, `plan_canceled_at` (soft migration). Lifecycle handlers: `subscription_created/updated/resumed/unpaused` re-derive plan from variant_id (handles tier upgrades); `subscription_cancelled/paused` keeps plan + stamps `plan_canceled_at` (sub stays active till renews_at); `subscription_expired` → plan='expired', clears sub_id; payment events log-only)_
- [x] **M3.6.4** Frontend: `/upgrade` page with Stripe Checkout link — M _(folded into the Account page Plan section instead of a separate `/upgrade` route — simpler UX. New `PLAN_TIERS` config with monthly/annual toggle (20% off badge), tier cards with Current/Recommended badges, Subscribe/Switch buttons. PaywallModal "Upgrade" CTA triggers same `createCheckoutApi` flow. `/account?checkout=success` redirect post-payment fires a toast + refreshes plan. New `POST /api/me/checkout` mints LSQ hosted-checkout URL with Clerk user email pre-filled and our `user_id` in `custom_data`. New `GET /api/me/portal` returns the LSQ self-service URL (404 when no customer_id))_
- [-] **M3.6.5** Test mode only; flip to live before launch — — S _(deferred — current variants are test-mode (USD; payments don't actually charge). Flip to live mode by creating live variants in LSQ + swapping IDs in env. No code change. Same applies to webhook secret — LSQ has separate signing secrets for test/live)_

**M3.6 open threads (2026-04-26):**

1. **LSQ store activation pending** — customer portal returns "This store has not been activated" because LSQ requires KYC docs (PAN/GST/business address) before exposing customer-facing portal pages. User submitted docs; awaiting LSQ approval. **Workaround until then**: cancel/manage subs via LSQ admin dashboard directly (Customers → click sub → Cancel) — fires the same webhook events.
2. **End-to-end webhook flow not yet verified live** — backend endpoint is reachable (returns 401 on bad sig confirming it ran), but no real LSQ event has been observed flipping `user_settings` post-deployment. We backfilled the user's first subscription manually. Will be verified the first time the user cancels/upgrades a sub via LSQ admin (or via portal once activated).
3. **JWT-paste pitfall fixed but worth flagging** — copy-paste of long secrets into Render dashboard picked up trailing newlines, producing `LocalProtocolError: Illegal header value`. Defensive `.strip()` added to all secret env-var reads (LSQ_API_KEY, LSQ_WEBHOOK_SECRET, CLERK_SECRET_KEY, RESEND_API_KEY) so future paste errors don't manifest as 500s.

## M3.9 R2 file storage

- [x] **M3.9.1** Cloudflare R2 bucket + API token — — S _(bucket `storyforge` provisioned; Object-RW token scoped to it; account/access/secret in gitignored `backend/.env` as `R2_ACCOUNT_ID` / `R2_ACCESS_KEY_ID` / `R2_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY` / `R2_BUCKET`. Verified with put/get/delete round-trip via boto3 before any code changes)_
- [x] **M3.9.2** Backend uploads source files to R2 instead of local disk — `routers/extractions.py` — M _(new [services/storage.py](backend/services/storage.py) wrapping boto3 (S3-compatible), env-gated. `save_upload` switches on `R2_BUCKET` — set → upload to `<bucket>/<extraction_id>/<safe_name>` and persist `r2://<bucket>/<key>`; unset → existing local-disk path. New `remove_upload(path)` branches the same way for cleanup; `delete_extraction` calls it post-commit and also nulls the `usage_log.extraction_id` FK so cost history outlives the artifact (Postgres enforces FK strictly, unlike SQLite default — was a latent bug exposed by the M3.2 Postgres swap). New dep: `boto3>=1.34.0`)_
- [x] **M3.9.3** Pre-signed URLs for source download — — S _(`/api/extractions/{id}/source` returns a 302 redirect to a presigned GET URL when the path is `r2://`, with `Cache-Control: no-store` so a stale URL doesn't survive past the 15-minute presign window. Browser fetches direct from R2 — zero egress cost. Local-disk paths still get FileResponse for dev parity. GDPR export ([routers/me.py](backend/routers/me.py)) also handles R2: downloads each source from R2 once and inlines it into the ZIP, falling back to direct file write for local paths)_

## M6.5 Notion export
- [x] **M6.5.1** Integration token (no OAuth); database picker (only sees databases the user explicitly shared with the integration); story → page with title in the database's title column (discovered from schema) + body rendered as Notion blocks (paragraph / heading_3 / bulleted_list_item / quote) — `backend/services/notion.py`, `backend/routers/integrations.py`, `frontend/src/components/PushToNotionModal.jsx`, `Settings.jsx`, `TopBar.jsx` — M
- [x] **M6.5.b** Property mapping UI — `NotionClient.get_database_schema(id)`; new `GET /api/integrations/notion/databases/{id}/schema`; `PushToNotionRequest.property_map` routes story fields (actor/want/so_that/section/source_quote/criteria) into Notion columns; mapped fields skipped from body to avoid duplication; per-field dropdown filtered by compatible Notion types in the push modal — `backend/services/notion.py`, `backend/routers/integrations.py`, `backend/models.py`, `frontend/src/components/PushToNotionModal.jsx`, `frontend/src/api.js` — M

## M6.6 Slack send-gaps-to-channel
- [x] **M6.6.1** Incoming webhook (no OAuth); channel is baked into the URL (one webhook = one channel); Block Kit message with severity badges + question + context; defaults to unresolved gaps only — `backend/services/slack.py`, `backend/routers/integrations.py`, `frontend/src/components/PushToSlackModal.jsx`, `Settings.jsx`, `TopBar.jsx` — S
- [x] **M6.6.b** Multi-webhook (named destinations: "dev-team", "stakeholders") — additional list inside Slack `config_json`; new `GET/POST/DELETE /api/integrations/slack/webhooks`; PushToSlackRequest accepts `webhook_id?`; Settings adds an "Additional destinations" section; push modal shows a destination picker (only when 2+ exist) — `backend/routers/integrations.py`, `backend/models.py`, `backend/services/slack.py` (unchanged), `frontend/src/api.js`, `frontend/src/components/PushToSlackModal.jsx`, `frontend/src/pages/Settings.jsx` — S

## M6.7 Public API + tokens
- [x] **M6.7.1** Long-lived bearer tokens (`sk_live_…`) for programmatic access; SHA-256-hashed at rest, plaintext shown once on creation; `current_user` dep dispatches by prefix (`sk_*` → token lookup; otherwise → Clerk JWT) so all existing routes work transparently with both — `backend/db/models.py`, `backend/services/api_tokens.py`, `backend/auth/deps.py`, `backend/routers/api_tokens.py`, `frontend/src/pages/Settings.jsx` — M
- [x] **M6.7.b** Read-only token scope — `ApiToken.scope` column ('rw'|'ro', default 'rw' for back-compat); `enforce_token_scope` dep blocks non-safe methods (POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE) with 403 when scope='ro'; CurrentUser carries `token_scope`; Settings create form picks scope; per-token badge — `backend/db/models.py`, `backend/db/session.py` (soft migration), `backend/auth/deps.py`, `backend/main.py`, `backend/routers/api_tokens.py`, `backend/models.py`, `frontend/src/pages/Settings.jsx`, `frontend/src/api.js` — S
- [x] **M6.7.c** Per-token rate limiting — in-process fixed-window counter keyed by token id, default 60 req/min (configurable via `STORYFORGE_API_RATE_LIMIT_PER_MINUTE`); 429 with `Retry-After` on hit; Clerk sessions skip the check — `backend/services/rate_limit.py`, `backend/auth/deps.py`, `backend/main.py` — S
- [x] **M6.7.d** OpenAPI spec page at /api-docs — Swagger UI moved to `/api-docs`; custom OpenAPI generator declares a `BearerAuth` security scheme so the Authorize button works; redoc disabled; Settings links to it from the API-tokens example block — `backend/main.py`, `frontend/src/pages/Settings.jsx` — M

Source-file persistence (R2) skipped when N > 1. UI shows multi-file staging list — `backend/services/ingest.py`, `backend/main.py`, `frontend/src/components/EmptyState.jsx`, `frontend/src/api.js` — M

Prompt updated to populate from `===== DOC i: name =====` markers. Additive — nothing visual changes; M10.2 + M10.3 build on these — `frontend/src/styles.css` — S

SignIn + SignUp pages get the brand mark + hero treatment so the entry pages read as StoryForge. ## M10.4 Color audit

Visual restraint: one brand accent dominates instead of decorative color sprawl — `frontend/src/components/ArtifactsPane.jsx`, `frontend/src/components/GapsRail.jsx`, `frontend/src/components/EmptyState.jsx`, `frontend/src/components/TopBar.jsx`, `frontend/src/pages/CompareView.jsx`, `frontend/src/pages/Account.jsx`, `frontend/src/pages/Settings.jsx` — S

# M14 — Lucid: Document Understanding Dossier (Phase 14)

> Pivot from "BRD → user stories" to "any document → narrated dossier (4-act story arc)". Phase 14 unfolds across ~5 build phases (foundation → annotations → structured extracts → conversational layer → personalisation). M14.0 is the brand swap; M14.1 is the dossier foundation; subsequent sub-milestones layer on annotations, chat, and stakeholder views.

## M14.0 Rebrand StoryForge → Lucid
- [x] **M14.0.1** Rebrand all user-facing surfaces from "StoryForge" to "Lucid".

## M14.1 Dossier foundation (lens architecture + dossier prompt + schema)
- [x] **M14.1.a** Backend lens architecture refactor — adds `lens` + `lens_payload` columns to `Extraction` (soft migration); creates `services/lenses/` registry pattern with `stories` (back-compat wrapper around existing extract_requirements) + `dossier` (new `DocumentDossier` Pydantic schema with 4-act narrative arc — overture, 14 sections, bridges between every section, closing — and `extract_dossier` function with master prompt). `call_claude` accepts `lens` param (default 'stories' for back-compat at the Python layer; routes default to 'dossier' for new uploads). New `persist_dossier_extraction` writes lens_payload + folds dossier.user_stories back into the legacy `stories` column. `/api/extract` accepts `lens` form param. `ExtractionRecord` Pydantic schema gains `lens` + `lens_payload` fields so frontend dispatchable. End-to-end round-trip smoke verified for both lenses; all 26 backend tests still pass — `backend/db/models.py`, `backend/db/session.py`, `backend/services/lenses/` (new), `backend/services/extractions.py`, `backend/main.py`, `backend/models.py` — M
- [x] **M14.1.b** Frontend dispatch + DossierPane skeleton renderer. New `frontend/src/components/dossier/DossierPane.jsx` — single-file component (~700 lines, lazy-loaded, ~4 KB gzipped) renders all 14 dossier sections + bridges + overture + closing in scroll order with a sticky 4-chapter nav (I · II · III · IV). Section components inline: BriefSection, TLDRLadder (3 reading depths), FiveW1H (6-cell grid), Glossary (term + definition table), MindmapTree (3-level nested ASCII-art tree), DomainGrid (7-card grid), SystemsView (entities + flows + feedback loops), FiveWhys (numbered chain with optional source quote), AssumptionsAudit (cards with risk-tone pills — high/med/low), InversionList (× failure scenarios), BetterQuestions (numbered list with "why it matters"), ActionItems (owner / action / when table), DecisionsRecord (made + open subsections), WhatToRevisit (numbered priority list), UserStoriesSection (folded-in stories from M14.0 pick (b) — only renders when populated). Bridges render as italic centred narrator text with thin horizontal rules either side. Overture as italic large display-font quote with accent-tinted gradient background. Closing as italic centred line. **App dispatch** ([App.jsx](frontend/src/App.jsx)): new branch — when `extraction.lens === 'dossier'` mount full-width DossierPane (no SourcePane / no ResizeHandle / no GapsRail since those are stories-shape concepts); otherwise existing dual-pane studio renders. Side GapsRail also gated on `lens !== 'dossier'`. **handleExtract** branches on lens: 'dossier' uses non-streaming `extract()` (POST /api/extract) since the streaming endpoint is still wired to the stories pipeline; 'stories' keeps the existing `extractStream()` path with usage ticks. Default lens for new uploads is 'dossier'. **api.js** `buildExtractForm` + `extract()` + `extractStream()` accept optional `lens` param, append to FormData when set — `frontend/src/api.js`, `frontend/src/App.jsx`, `frontend/src/components/dossier/DossierPane.jsx` (new) — L
- [x] **M14.1.c** Streaming integration for dossier + scrollspy chapter nav. New `services/streaming_dossier.stream_dossier_extraction` mirrors stories streaming via Anthropic tool-use `messages.stream()` (DocumentDossier as tool input_schema, MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS bumped to 16k for the bigger schema). Same SSE event shape (start/usage/complete/error) so the frontend doesn't need to know about the lens. `/api/extract/stream` accepts `lens` form param + branches the streamer + persister. Frontend `handleExtract` now uses `extractStream({lens:'dossier'})` for both lenses (no more non-streaming branch); LoadingState progress card animates for dossier too. DossierPane gains scrollspy via IntersectionObserver (root=scroller-ref, rootMargin top-third); ChapterNav highlights the active chapter pill with accent-soft bg + accent border + accent-ink text — `backend/services/streaming_dossier.py` (new), `backend/main.py`, `frontend/src/App.jsx`, `frontend/src/components/dossier/DossierPane.jsx` — M

## M14.5 Notion-clean design refresh (in-app workspace surfaces)
- [x] **M14.5.f** Account page exact-replica from screenshot. **Page header**: 56px User IconTile + serif "Account" + subtitle ("Manage your profile, usage, activity and subscription"). **KPI strip**: 4 cards in a responsive grid (single column < 640px, 2 cols < 980px, 4 cols above) — Tokens used (Activity icon + big number + "of 1,000,000" + progress bar with % label), Total cost (DollarSign icon + dollar value + "This billing cycle"), Extractions (Box icon + count + "This month"), Plan (Calendar icon + plan name + renews date). Each card has icon disc top-left + Info icon top-right + label + big serif number + sublabel. Tokens-used card has a horizontal progress bar with teal gradient fill. **Usage card**: Activity IconTile + "Usage" title + subtitle, with a decorative SVG sparkline preview on the right (15-point line + accent-tinted area gradient + endpoint dot — purely cosmetic, real per-day chart is later work) + body wraps existing UsageSection. **Recent activity card**: 2-col layout — left has Clock IconTile + title + subtitle, right has the existing RecentActivitySection (limited to ~3 entries via the existing component's behavior). **Plan & subscription card**: SettingsIcon + title + body wraps existing PlanSection (which already has the monthly/annual toggle + tier rows). **Data + Profile cards**: same AccountCard wrapper. New icons added: Calendar, Clock, Box. New CSS class `.account-kpi-row` for responsive 4-col → 2-col → 1-col KPI grid. - [x] **M14.5.b** EmptyState complete redesign — addresses 10-point UX critique. **Layout shift**: page is now three vertical zones — (1) Hero + Upload card side-by-side at >= 980px, (2) "What you'll get" 8-card grid, (3) Quick-start templates + trust strip. Page no longer has dead vertical space — every below-the-fold pixel earns its keep. **Hero** ([components/EmptyState.jsx](frontend/src/components/EmptyState.jsx)): smaller, less prominent. New copy: "Upload a messy requirement. Get structured stories, gaps, NFRs, and acceptance criteria — in minutes." Subhead pivoted to value + verification: "Lucid reads your document like an expert analyst. Every artifact links back to the source quote, so you can verify and push to Jira in one click." "Powered by Claude Opus 4.7" demoted from headline-adjacent badge to a single line in the trust strip at the bottom. **Upload card** beefed up substantially: tab strip at top (Upload file / Paste text — with the active tab pill in white-on-bg-subtle and an icon), drop zone OR textarea swap based on tab, **Output type dropdown** replacing the cryptic "mode: extract" chip (Full dossier / User stories only — both wired to lens param; "BRD summary / Gap analysis / Technical spec" listed as `(soon)` disabled options so the roadmap is visible). **Primary CTA** now a solid teal full-width button with shadow + outcome-driven copy "Analyze document" + Send icon. Disabled state is muted but the active state has visual weight + a colored shadow. **What you'll get** section: 8 artifact cards in a flexible grid (Brief, 5W1H, Mindmap, User Stories, NFRs, Gaps & Risks, Action Items, Better Questions) with icon disc + title + 1-line description — sets expectations BEFORE the user invests in uploading. **Quick-start templates**: 3 sample buttons (Sample BRD — Loyalty program; Meeting notes — Payment gateway replacement; Email thread — API integration feedback) — click loads a realistic sample into the paste textarea so the user can try Lucid without finding a doc first. Sample texts are static strings (~250-450 chars each). **Trust strip**: 5 inline pills at the bottom — Source-grounded · Gap detection · One-click push to Jira/Linear/Notion · Export Word/Excel/Markdown/JSON · Powered by Claude. **Sidebar update** ([components/Sidebar.jsx](frontend/src/components/Sidebar.jsx)): added "New Extraction" item at the top of the WORKSPACE group, linked to `/`, so users on the upload page see a clearly active sidebar item (was: nothing active when on `/`). Existing solid-accent-pill active styling from M12.1 makes it visually clear. **App.jsx** ([App.jsx](frontend/src/App.jsx)): `handleExtract` now reads `lens` from the EmptyState submit payload (was hardcoded `'dossier'`); falls back to dossier when not specified. **Trade-offs**: rewriting EmptyState end-to-end means the previous "How it works" 3-card grid + the gradient hero are gone — the new layout doesn't need them because the value prop is communicated via "What you'll get" + the trust strip. Modes that don't exist yet are visible as disabled options — risks the user thinking they're broken; mitigated by the `(soon)` suffix. Sample texts are hardcoded English; could add per-locale samples later. Sidebar's "New Extraction" item duplicates the brand-row "Edit" icon button (which already does new-extraction); deliberate, because the brand-row icon is unlabeled and easy to miss — the sidebar nav item is the "primary" path. **Build**: 4 vitest + vite clean. EmptyState chunk grew (more content + sample text), but it's part of the main bundle (not lazy), so this lives in `index-*.js` rather than a chunk. **Not browser-verified** — recommend smoke (sign in → confirm new EmptyState layout: hero left + upload right at desktop width → resize narrow → confirm stacks → click "Sample BRD" → confirm textarea fills + tab swaps to Paste → click Analyze → confirm extraction runs → switch dropdown to "User stories only" → re-run → confirm stories pane renders → check sidebar: "New Extraction" item shows active accent pill on `/`).
- [x] **M14.5.a** Design-token + DossierPane refresh — in-app workspace surfaces switch from "early-SaaS warm-cream + bordered/shadowed cards + heavy gradients" to "Notion-clean: pure white + paper-thin borders + near-zero shadows + serif as accent only". Reference: Notion Ramp HQ kanban screenshot. **Token changes** ([styles.css](frontend/src/styles.css)): `--bg` warm-cream `#faf9f6` → near-white `#fcfcfb`; `--bg-subtle` warm `#f4f3ef` → cool `#f7f7f5`; `--bg-hover` `#f0eeea` → `#f1f1ee`; `--border` warm `#e5e3dd` → cool `#ebebe7`; `--border-strong` similarly; shadow scale dialed back ~30-40% (`--shadow-xs` 0.04 → 0.025 alpha; `--shadow-lg` from layered to single-shadow); `--gradient-soft` dropped from 0.06-0.08 alpha to 0.018-0.025 alpha (now reads as ambient light, not decoration). Marketing surfaces (Landing, SignIn) untouched — they keep their own `--lp-*` palette per M13. **DossierPane refresh** ([components/dossier/DossierPane.jsx](frontend/src/components/dossier/DossierPane.jsx)): paneShell background switched from page-tint to pure white (was `var(--surface-0)`, now `var(--bg-elevated)`). contentColumn now `clamp()`-fluid: `maxWidth: min(960px, 92vw)` + `padding: clamp(32px, 5vw, 64px) clamp(20px, 4vw, 48px) 120px` so content reflows smoothly across viewports instead of dead-spacing on wide monitors. Section gap 24 → 32px for breathing room. **SectionShell flattened** — was a bordered/shadowed white card on tinted page; now sections sit directly on the page surface with just a section title + breathing whitespace. Reads as long-form document rather than stacked widgets — Notion's page-as-canvas pattern. **Overture** — was a chunky padded card with gradient bg + 3px accent border; now a simple 2px accent left-border + italic serif text, no card chrome. **Bridges** — were italic text between two thin horizontal rules; now bare italic centred line in display font (the rules added visual noise with no semantic value). **Chapter headers** — Roman + title moved from muted-grey to teal accent uppercase mini-label; intro paragraph in serif italic for the narrative voice. Section spacing within a chapter widened 24 → 36px. **ChapterNav refined** — pills lost their borders (was bordered chips); active state uses subtle `--bg-hover` background only (no border, no accent-soft fill). Backdrop-blur bumped 6→8px; mini-Roman numeral font-weight & color refined. **Closing** — extra top spacing + bigger fluid font. **Trade-offs**: the lighter shadows + flatter cards mean the dossier looks more like a Word document than an app surface — that's the point but if it reads as "too plain" the section title weight or a subtle accent border-left can come back. Reading width 960px is wider than the previous 820 — slightly looser line-length but reads correctly on 13-32" screens via clamp(). The overture lost its visual punch; if users miss the gradient-bg version, easy revert. Marketing surfaces (Landing, SignIn) deliberately keep their decorative palette — they're brand moments, not workspace. **What's NOT changed in this commit** (deferred to M14.5.b if user wants more): Account/Documents/Settings PageShell padding standardization; TopBar chrome (badges, version chips); side rails; Sidebar tone refinements (already close to Notion-style after M12.1). **Build**: 4 vitest + vite clean. DossierPane chunk 32.89 → 32.64 KB (slight shrink — removed gradients, simpler card markup) — `frontend/src/styles.css`, `frontend/src/components/dossier/DossierPane.jsx` — L

## M14.4 Conversational layer (chat with the document)
- [x] **M14.4.a** Per-extraction chat — turns Lucid from a destination ("read the dossier, leave") into a workspace ("read the dossier, ask follow-ups, draft responses, run what-ifs"). **Backend**: new `ChatMessage` table ([db/models.py](backend/db/models.py)) — composite of `(extraction_id, user_id, role, content, model_used, tokens)` with timestamps. New service `services/chat.chat_stream` ([services/chat.py](backend/services/chat.py) — new) — Claude `messages.stream()` with system block = persona + full `extraction.raw_text` + a compact dossier digest (just the high-signal bits: overture / brief / numbers / 5W1H / assumptions / inversion / negative space / actions / open decisions — keeps the digest under ~2k tokens). System block is `cache_control: ephemeral` so follow-up messages within 5 min hit prompt cache (~10× cheaper). Defaults to Sonnet 4.6 (cheaper / faster than Opus, plenty smart for Q&A over an already-extracted doc). NO RAG / embeddings — most docs fit Claude's 1M context, simpler to ship; can layer chunk + embed later without changing the public chat_stream signature. New router `routers/chat.py` ([routers/chat.py](backend/routers/chat.py) — new) — `GET /chat` lists thread, `POST /chat` persists user msg + streams assistant via SSE + persists assistant on `complete`, `DELETE /chat` clears. Same `_owned_extraction` ownership check as the rest of /api/extractions. Mounted in main.py with the same `_protected_deps` posture. **Frontend**: `api.js` gets `listChatMessagesApi` / `sendChatMessageStream` / `clearChatApi`. New `components/dossier/ChatPanel.jsx` (~280 lines) — fixed-position floating pane in the studio's bottom-right, two states: collapsed pill ("💬 Ask anything about this document") and expanded panel (header + message list + starter chip row + input). Streaming text grows in a "live" assistant bubble with a blinking cursor; on `complete` it reconciles with the persisted message. Auto-scroll to bottom on new messages. Cmd/Ctrl+Enter handled via `Enter` (Shift+Enter for newline). Three starter prompts as one-click chips — "Draft response" / "Meeting prep" / "What if" — fire pre-templated questions through the same pipeline (drafters as prompt templates, not separate routes; M14.4.b can promote them to dedicated UI if needed). Mounted in DossierPane as a fixed overlay so it doesn't affect dossier scroll layout — `backend/db/models.py`, `backend/services/chat.py` (new), `backend/routers/chat.py` (new), `backend/main.py`, `frontend/src/api.js`, `frontend/src/components/dossier/ChatPanel.jsx` (new), `frontend/src/components/dossier/DossierPane.jsx`, `frontend/src/styles.css` — XL

## M14.3 Structured extracts (Numbers + Negative Space + Timeline)
- [x] **M14.3.a** Three new dossier sections that all share the "extend the schema with new structured fields" pattern. Backend ([services/lenses/dossier.py](backend/services/lenses/dossier.py)): three new Pydantic models — `NumbersExtract` (list of `NumberFact { label, value, category, source }` covering cost / time / count / percentage / other), `Timeline` (list of `TimelinePhase { label, when, description }`), `NegativeSpace` (list of `NegativeSpaceItem { missing_item, why_it_matters }` — what the doc DOESN'T say). Three new top-level fields on `DocumentDossier` with `default_factory=` so old dossiers parse cleanly. Six new bridges inserted at the right narrative points: Brief→Numbers→TLDR (Act I); Domain→Timeline→Systems (Act II); Inversion→NegativeSpace→Better Questions (Act III). Legacy bridges (`bridge_brief_to_tldr`, `bridge_domain_to_systems`, `bridge_inversion_to_questions`) kept on the schema with `default=""` for backward-compat with pre-M14.3 saved dossiers; new dossiers leave them empty per prompt instruction. Master prompt updated with explicit rules for each new section + a "use new bridges, leave legacy empty" instruction. Mock dossier populates all three so dev mode renders end-to-end. Frontend ([components/dossier/DossierPane.jsx](frontend/src/components/dossier/DossierPane.jsx)): three new section renderers — `NumbersExtractSection` (table grouped by category, mono-font values, optional SourceQuote per row + ConfidenceBadge), `TimelineGantt` (alternating accent-tone phase header strip + numbered phase list with description), `NegativeSpaceList` (∅ symbol bullet + missing item + why-it-matters). Dispatch is conditional — when a section's payload is empty the act falls through to the legacy bridge (preserves old dossier rendering). All three new sections use the M14.2 annotation primitives (GlossaryTermified for prose, SourceQuote where applicable) — `backend/services/lenses/dossier.py`, `frontend/src/components/dossier/DossierPane.jsx` — L

## M14.2 Dossier annotations (provenance + glossary tooltips + confidence labels)
- [x] **M14.2.a** Three annotation primitives applied across every prose section of the dossier — no backend / schema / prompt changes, all client-side over data the existing dossier already carries. New `frontend/src/components/dossier/annotations.jsx` with three small components: `<GlossaryTermified text terms>` (regex-walks text, substitutes hover-tooltip spans for any glossary term — case-sensitive word-boundary match, longer terms win first to avoid "Story" preempting "User Story"; native `title` attribute for the popover, no popover lib, dotted-underline + accent-tinted color signals "hover for more"); `<SourceQuote text>` (compact `<details>` disclosure — "View source" expands to show the verbatim quote in an accent-soft blockquote); `<ConfidenceBadge sourced>` (tiny pill — "✓ Sourced" green when item has a source quote, "Asserted" muted when synthesized; clicking has no action — informational). Wired into DossierPane: every prose-bearing section (Brief, TLDR Ladder, 5W1H, Domain branches, Systems entities/flows/loops, 5 Whys, Assumptions, Inversion, Better Questions, Action Items, Decisions, What to Revisit, User Stories) wraps text in `<GlossaryTermified terms={glossaryTerms}>`. Sections with source-quote fields (5 Whys evidence, Action Items source, User Stories source_quote) gain the SourceQuote disclosure + ConfidenceBadge — `frontend/src/components/dossier/annotations.jsx` (new), `frontend/src/components/dossier/DossierPane.jsx` — M
