All 26 tests green in 1.8s. **CI** ([.github/workflows/ci.yml](.github/workflows/ci.yml)): single workflow with two jobs — backend runs `pytest -v` on Python 3.13 with pip caching; frontend runs `npm run build` on Node 20 with npm caching + a `pk_test_ci_placeholder_key` so Vite's import-time check on `VITE_CLERK_PUBLISHABLE_KEY` doesn't crash. Triggers on push to main + all PRs. Branch-protect rule (M0.2.4) deferred — toggle in repo settings, no code. **Observability** ([backend/services/obs.py](backend/services/obs.py)): three primitives in one module so wiring stays minimal in main.py. `JsonFormatter` emits one-line JSON per record with ts/level/logger/msg + rid + exc — fields Render's log pipeline can index, vs grep on a pretty string. `RequestIdMiddleware` mints `uuid4().hex[:12]` (or trusts inbound `X-Request-Id` for trace-correlation), binds to a `ContextVar` so the formatter auto-attaches the id to every log line for that request, echoes it back as a response header, and emits a single access-log line per request (`POST /api/extract -> 200 in 124.3ms`). `install_sentry()` is silent no-op when `SENTRY_DSN` is unset (so dev + preview branches never break for lack of creds); when set, initializes `sentry-sdk` with `FastApiIntegration` (auto-captures HTTPExceptions) + `LoggingIntegration(event_level=ERROR)` so `log.exception()` lands in Sentry too. Trace sampling default 0; flip via `SENTRY_TRACES_SAMPLE_RATE`. `send_default_pii=False`. main.py installs JSON logging + Sentry *before* FastAPI construction (so import-time log lines + startup errors go through the pipeline) and request-id middleware *before* CORS (so OPTIONS preflights also get an id — useful when debugging cross-origin failures). **Frontend Sentry, Vitest+RTL, Playwright, PostHog, coverage gate, anthropic token usage logging** all deferred to dedicated milestones — current scope was the foundation, not the full M0 surface. **Smoke ✓**: full pytest suite green; obs module imports cleanly; main.py boots without sentry-sdk crash when `SENTRY_DSN` unset.
- **2026-04-25 · M3.6 (M3.6.1 → M3.6.4, M3.6.5 deferred)** Lemon Squeezy billing wired end-to-end. **Why LSQ not Stripe**: per [DECISIONS.md → D6](DECISIONS.md), Stripe is invitation-only in India; LSQ is a Merchant of Record (handles VAT/GST in customer's jurisdiction, settles USD to Indian bank). 5% + $0.50 fee absorbed in margin per D5 strategy update. **Setup**: store `The Growth Mentor` (id 355995, USD currency, country IN), 6 published variants matching DECISIONS exactly (Starter/Pro/Team × monthly/annual). 9 env vars in gitignored `backend/.env`. Test-mode creds; flipping to live = swap variant IDs + webhook secret, no code change. **Backend**: new [services/lsq.py](backend/services/lsq.py) wraps LSQ REST (httpx, no SDK — keeps mocks easier). Helpers: `variant_for(tier, interval)` env lookup, `variant_to_plan(variant_id)` reverse, `create_checkout_url(target, user_id, email, name)` mints hosted-checkout pre-filled with email + `custom_data.user_id` for webhook attribution, `customer_portal_url(customer_id)` reads the long-lived signed portal URL from LSQ's customer resource. New [routers/billing.py](backend/routers/billing.py): `POST /api/me/checkout` (Clerk-authed; returns LSQ URL), `GET /api/me/portal` (Clerk-authed; 404 when no `lsq_customer_id`), `POST /api/webhooks/lemonsqueezy` (UN-authed, HMAC-SHA256 verified, raw body before parsing so sig matches what LSQ signed). Lifecycle handlers cover `subscription_created` / `_updated` / `_cancelled` / `_paused` / `_resumed` / `_unpaused` / `_expired`; payment events log-only; missing `user_id` returns 200 noop (LSQ won't retry). Webhooks always 200 on parse-success so unknown future events don't trigger retry storms. **Schema**: `user_settings` gains 4 columns — `lsq_customer_id`, `lsq_subscription_id`, `plan_renews_at`, `plan_canceled_at` (soft migration on both SQLite and Postgres). `/api/me/plan` extended to surface subscription state for the Account UI. **Frontend**: [api.js](frontend/src/api.js) gains `createCheckoutApi({tier, interval})` + `getPortalApi()`. [PaywallModal](frontend/src/components/PaywallModal.jsx) "Upgrade" button now mints LSQ checkout + `window.location` (no popup, no iframe, no CSP gymnastics) + adds a "See all plans" secondary going to /account. New `PlanSection` in [Account page](frontend/src/pages/Account.jsx) replaces the placeholder: badge with current plan + renewal/cancellation date, monthly/annual toggle (20% off badge), tier cards with Current/Recommended badges + Subscribe/Switch buttons, Manage subscription button when `has_active_subscription`. `?checkout=success` query param fires a toast + refreshes plan + strips the query so refresh doesn't re-toast. **Smoke ✓ 11/11**: variant resolution forward + reverse, **real LSQ checkout URL minted** (`https://thegrowthmentor.lemonsqueezy.com/checkout/custom/...`), portal 404 when no sub, webhook signature verification (rejects bad sig 401), full lifecycle (created → active starter; updated → upgraded to pro; cancelled → keeps pro + stamps canceled_at; expired → 'expired' + clears sub_id), missing user_id → noop 200. 34-assertion isolation test still green. Build clean (121 modules, 111 KB JS gzipped).
- **2026-04-25 · M3.5 (M3.5.4 + .5 + .6)** Free-tier limits + sidebar usage bar + paywall modal. Implementation follows DECISIONS.md exactly. **Schema**: `user_settings.plan` (varchar, indexed, default null=trial) + `trial_ends_at` (timestamp) — soft migration runs on both SQLite and Postgres. **Tier table** lives in [services/plans.py](backend/services/plans.py) as the single source of truth: Trial (10 total, Sonnet, 200k chars / ~25pg), Starter $20 (25/mo, Sonnet, same cap), Pro $49 (100/mo, Sonnet+Opus, 400k chars / ~50pg), Team $99 (300/mo, all models, 800k chars / ~100pg), plus an `expired` sentinel that fails every gate. Doc-size cap is in *characters* not tokens because Anthropic doesn't ship a tokenizer; conservative ~4 chars/token conversion. **Gating**: new [services/limits.py](backend/services/limits.py) `enforce_limits()` runs in `/api/extract` + `/rerun` *before* the Claude call (no token burn on doomed requests). Four gates in order — trial expiry → 403 (also auto-flips plan to 'expired' as a side-effect), model not allowed → 403, doc too large → 413, monthly cap → 429. All raise `HTTPException(detail={paywall: true, reason, current_plan, upgrade_to, message, ...reason-specific extras})`. Naive datetimes coming back from SQLite/Postgres `TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE` are coerced UTC via a tiny `_aware()` helper. **Trial init**: extended [services/onboarding.py](backend/services/onboarding.py) `welcome_check` to also set `plan='trial'` + `trial_ends_at = now + 14d` on first authed touch (folded into the existing welcome path so no extra DB hits). **New endpoint**: `GET /api/me/plan` returns `{plan, plan_name, extractions_per_period, usage_in_period, max_input_chars, allowed_models, upgrade_to, trial_ends_at, period_resets_at, period_label}` — paid plans use calendar month with first-of-next-month reset; trial uses trial-period total with `trial_ends_at` reset. **Frontend**: [api.js](frontend/src/api.js) `jsonOrThrow` extracts `body.detail.paywall=true` payloads onto `err.paywall` so callers branch without re-parsing message strings. New `getMePlanApi()` client. [App.jsx](frontend/src/App.jsx) caches `plan` in state, refreshes on mount + org-switch + after every successful extract/rerun, exposes via AppContext alongside `showPaywall(payload)` imperative trigger. New [components/PaywallModal.jsx](frontend/src/components/PaywallModal.jsx) renders a scrim + dialog with reason-specific icon/title, the human message, reason-specific extra context (current_usage/limit for monthly_limit; doc_pages_estimate for doc_too_large), and an "Upgrade to {tier}" CTA navigating to `/account`. Esc + click-outside dismiss. New `UsageBar` in [Sidebar](frontend/src/components/Sidebar.jsx) between the nav and UserPill: tier-toned badge, monospace count `{used}/{limit}`, thin progress bar (accent → warn at 80% → danger at 100%), upgrade hint when ≥80%; click → `/account`. **Smoke ✓ all 4 gates** via dependency-override TestClient: model-not-allowed (Opus on Trial → 403, upgrade_to=starter), doc-too-large (300k chars → 413, max_pages=100), monthly-limit (10/10 mock rows → 429), trial-expired (back-dated trial_ends_at → 403, plan auto-flipped to 'expired'); happy-path (Starter, small doc, Sonnet → 200, /plan reflects 1/25). 34-assertion isolation test still green. Build clean (121 modules, 110 KB JS gzipped).
- **2026-04-25 · M3.10 (M3.10.2 + M3.10.3, M3.10.1 superseded, M3.10.4 deferred)** Render single-container deploy, no Vercel split. **Decision**: skipping the split-architecture (Vercel SPA + Render backend) saves a CORS allowlist, two URLs to manage, two deploy pipelines — for the user's scale (free tier, single dev) one URL is the right call. Revisit Vercel later if SPA edge perf matters. **render.yaml** declares one web service, free plan, **Singapore** region (lowest latency from India), Docker runtime pointing at the existing multi-stage `Dockerfile` from M0, `healthCheckPath: /api/health` (unauth-protected per M3.1). All 13 secrets listed with `sync: false` so placeholders ship in git but real values get pasted into Render's Environment tab — `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`, `STORYFORGE_MODEL`, `STORYFORGE_MASTER_KEY`, `CLERK_SECRET_KEY`, `CLERK_PUBLISHABLE_KEY`, `DATABASE_URL`, `R2_ACCOUNT_ID`, `R2_ACCESS_KEY_ID`, `R2_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY`, `R2_BUCKET`, `RESEND_API_KEY`, `WELCOME_FROM_EMAIL`, `WELCOME_FROM_NAME`, plus `CORS_ORIGINS` (only matters if a third-party frontend ever calls in — single-container same-origin doesn't trigger CORS at runtime). **Dockerfile**: CMD switched to shell-form (`uvicorn ... --port ${PORT:-8000}`) so Render's auto-injected `PORT` actually expands; exec-form would crash with "invalid port: '${PORT:-8000}'". **Backend**: `main.py` CORS now reads `CORS_ORIGINS` env (comma-separated, additive on top of localhost dev defaults). **SPA fallback**: new `_SPAStaticFiles` subclass overrides `get_response` to fall back to `index.html` when StaticFiles 404s — modern Starlette raises `HTTPException` AND can return a 404 Response depending on path shape (trailing-slash redirects), handle both. Without this, direct loads of `/documents`, `/projects/:id`, `/account`, `/sign-in/*` would 404 in production. **Smoke ✓ via local Docker**: `docker build` clean (~30s); container runs on `PORT=9876`; `/` → 200 text/html; `/documents` → 200 text/html (SPA fallback works); `/sign-in` → 200 text/html; `/api/health` → 200; `/api/extractions` → 401 (auth gate intact); SQLite fallback fires when `DATABASE_URL` unset. **What's left for the user**: connect the GitHub repo in Render dashboard → click "Apply Blueprint" (Render reads `render.yaml`) → paste 13 env vars from local `backend/.env` → wait ~5 min for build → grab the live URL → add it to Clerk's "Allowed Origins" so sign-in works in prod (and to `CORS_ORIGINS` if needed). M3.10.4 (custom domain) deferred — `*.onrender.com` ships with valid SSL out of the box.
- **2026-04-25 · M3.7 (M3.7.1 + M3.7.2)** Welcome email via Resend, fired by **first-touch detection** instead of a Clerk webhook. **Architectural switch** from the original PROJECT.md plan: webhooks need a publicly-reachable backend URL (don't have one until M3.10) and a first-touch detector is functionally equivalent for users who actually open the app — if they never come back, why welcome them anyway? Webhook can be layered on top later as a second trigger; this code stays as the fallback. **Backend**: new [services/email.py](backend/services/email.py) wrapping Resend's REST API via httpx (no SDK — two endpoints, not worth the dep). Helpers: `send_welcome_email(to, name)`, `fetch_clerk_user(user_id)` (Clerk's session JWT doesn't carry email by default, so the welcome path needs a server-side lookup with the secret key), `primary_email_of(clerk_user)`. Hard 10-second timeout so a slow third party can't pile up uvicorn workers. New [services/onboarding.py](backend/services/onboarding.py) with `welcome_check` FastAPI dependency: PK lookup on `user_settings` → if `welcome_sent_at IS NULL`, set it to `now()` + commit + enqueue background task. **Mark-before-send pattern**: timestamp set BEFORE the network call so a transient Resend failure can't trigger send-loops on every subsequent request — accept the dropped welcome over send spam. Manual retrigger: `UPDATE user_settings SET welcome_sent_at = NULL`. Wired as a router-level `dependencies=[..., Depends(welcome_check)]` on extractions/projects/me, and explicitly on the inline `/api/extract` + `/api/test-key` routes so every protected endpoint contributes equally. Background task body runs after response is sent — Clerk fetch + Resend send happen off the request path. **Schema**: new `user_settings.welcome_sent_at` column (nullable, no index — only ever read via PK). Soft migration applied to both SQLite and Postgres. **Smoke ✓**: stubbed Clerk + Resend, asserted: first GET `/api/me/settings` by user A → 1 email + 1 Clerk lookup; 3 more requests → still 1 email (idempotent); first request by user B → 2nd email with B's address; `welcome_sent_at` persisted. 34-assertion isolation test still green. **Live email** to user's real Clerk-registered address fires on next browser refresh.
- **2026-04-25 · M3.9 (M3.9.1 → M3.9.3) + delete-cascade fix** Cloudflare R2 storage for source uploads, end-to-end. **Setup**: bucket `storyforge` + Object-RW API token (scoped to that bucket); `R2_*` env vars in gitignored `backend/.env`; new dep `boto3>=1.34.0`. Credentials verified via put/get/delete round-trip *before* any code changes. **Backend**: new [services/storage.py](backend/services/storage.py) wrapping boto3 (S3-compatible — R2 needs `signature_version='s3v4'` + `region_name='auto'`). Helpers: `is_enabled()`, `is_r2_path()`, `parse_r2_path()`, `make_r2_path()`, `upload_bytes()`, `presigned_get_url()` (15-min default TTL), `delete_path()`. **Persisted-path scheme**: `Extraction.source_file_path` is either an absolute local path (legacy + dev fallback) or `r2://<bucket>/<key>` (M3.9 onwards). [services/extractions.py](backend/services/extractions.py) `save_upload` env-gates on `R2_BUCKET`: set → upload to R2, return `r2://...`; unset → write to local disk, return absolute path. New `remove_upload(path)` branches for cleanup; `delete_extraction` calls it post-commit. **Surfaced + fixed an M3.2 latent bug**: Postgres enforces FK strictly (unlike SQLite default), so deleting an extraction would 500 because `usage_log.extraction_id` still referenced it. Per the original M3.0 design intent ("usage records what cost money even if the artifact is gone"), `delete_extraction` now NULLs the FK on every `usage_log` row before deleting the extraction — cost history outlives the artifact. **Source download**: `/api/extractions/{id}/source` returns 302 redirect to a presigned URL when the path is `r2://`, with `Cache-Control: no-store` so a stale URL can't survive past the 15-min presign window. Browser fetches direct from R2 — zero egress cost on Cloudflare. Local-disk paths keep using FileResponse. **GDPR export** ([routers/me.py](backend/routers/me.py)) also handles R2: downloads each source from R2 once and inlines it into the ZIP. **Smoke ✓ end-to-end against live R2 + Postgres**: extract w/ file → `source_file_path=r2://storyforge/ext_xxx/file.txt` → /source → 302 with valid SigV4 presigned URL → presigned URL fetches identical bytes → GDPR export ZIP includes the file → DELETE → R2 head_object 404 + usage_log retained with `extraction_id=NULL`. 34-assertion isolation test still green.

Personal context filter: `user_id=:uid AND org_id IS NULL`; org context filter: `org_id=:org_id` (every member sees every org row — workspace = shared, no per-user filter inside an org). `persist_extraction`/`record_usage` take `org_id`; `/api/extract` + `/rerun` set it from `user.org_id`. - **2026-04-24 · M3.1.2 → M3.1.7** Auth wired end-to-end. Unsigned-in visitors hit `/sign-in`; the rest of the app is locked behind a Clerk session. **Backend**: new [auth/clerk.py](backend/auth/clerk.py) verifies JWTs locally via PyJWT against the JWKS at `<derived-issuer>/.well-known/jwks.json` (issuer derived by base64-decoding the publishable key — same algorithm Clerk's frontend SDK uses). New dep: `pyjwt[crypto]>=2.8.0`. Deliberately *did not* use `clerk-sdk-python`/`clerk-backend-api` — JWKS verification is 30 lines of stable code, no point coupling to SDK release cadence. **Frontend**: `@clerk/clerk-react` v5.61.6 added. New CSS rule extends `.row-action` hover-reveal to `.doc-row` (so the new "…" button uses the same fade pattern as the trash button). Smoke test ✓: create 2 projects → extract → move to P1 → list filters correctly → rename P1 → move to P2 → remove → delete both projects → extraction survives with `project_id=None`. Build clean: 58 modules, 79.0KB JS / 2.0KB CSS gzipped.
- **2026-04-24 · M2.3 (M2.3.1 → M2.3.3)** Source-file storage. Uploads land at `backend/uploads/<extraction_id>/<safe_filename>` (extraction id minted up front so the disk write happens *before* persist — a write failure 500s without orphaning a row). New helpers in [services/extractions.py](backend/services/extractions.py): `_safe_filename` (strip path separators + control chars, fall back to "uploaded"), `upload_dir_for` (path-traversal guard via `Path.resolve()` + root-prefix check), `save_upload`, `remove_upload_dir`. New `STORYFORGE_UPLOAD_DIR` env var (default `backend/uploads`). New `GET /api/extractions/{id}/source` in [routers/extractions.py](backend/routers/extractions.py) returns `FileResponse` with `mimetypes.guess_type`-derived content-type; explicit registrations for `.md`/`.markdown`/`.rst` since the platform db varies by host. 404 covers all three "nothing to show" cases (missing row, paste-mode extraction, file vanished). `delete_extraction` now calls `remove_upload_dir` post-delete (best-effort, non-blocking — the row is already gone). Smoke test ✓: upload→/source returns identical bytes (76/76, `text/plain; charset=utf-8`)→delete→directory removed→/source 404; paste-mode extraction returns 404 on /source as expected. No frontend wiring yet — a "Download original" button in the studio is a separate task.
- **2026-04-24 · M2.2 (M2.2.1 → M2.2.7) + M2.4 (M2.4.1, .3, .4, .5)** Full backend↔frontend swap — Documents view is now server-backed. **Backend** — new [models.py](backend/models.py) request/response schemas (`ExtractionRecord`, `ExtractionSummary`, `ExtractionPatch`, `ExtractionImport`, `GapStateRead`, `GapStatePatch`, `ProjectRead/Create/Patch`); new [services/extractions.py](backend/services/extractions.py) with `_mint_id()` matching the JS shape (`<prefix>_<base36-ts>_<rand6>`), Pydantic↔SQLModel converters, `persist_extraction`, `delete_extraction` (manual gap-state cascade); new [routers/extractions.py](backend/routers/extractions.py) — list/get/patch/delete + per-gap upsert + `POST /import` (idempotent migration endpoint, returns existing row on duplicate id); new [routers/projects.py](backend/routers/projects.py) — CRUD where delete *detaches* extractions rather than cascading. [main.py](backend/main.py) /api/extract now persists every run, recording `model_used="mock"` when no key was set, and returns the full `ExtractionRecord` (with id) so the frontend never has to round-trip again. Smoke test ✓ end-to-end: project create→list→delete; extraction create (live Sonnet)→list summary→get full→patch filename→delete (404 after); gap-state upsert; import idempotency (re-POST same id returns 201 with existing row). **Frontend** — [api.js](frontend/src/api.js) rewritten as a typed client (`listExtractionsApi`, `getExtractionApi`, `patchExtractionApi`, `deleteExtractionApi`, `importExtractionApi`, `listGapStatesApi`, `patchGapStateApi`, project CRUD, `health`, `testApiKey`); errors now carry `.status` so callers can branch on 404. [lib/store.js](frontend/src/lib/store.js) is a thin async wrapper — `listExtractions/getExtraction/deleteExtraction/insertExtraction/getGapStates/setGapState`. New [lib/migrate.js](frontend/src/lib/migrate.js) runs once on boot, pushes any leftover `storyforge:extractions` records to `/api/extractions/import` preserving original ids, only clears local on full success, sticky `storyforge:migrated:v1` flag prevents reruns. [App.jsx](frontend/src/App.jsx) `restoreExtraction` now branches: full record (e.g. fresh extraction) opens immediately; summary row triggers `getExtraction(id)` and toasts on 404. New `useEffect` calls `migrateLocalStorageOnce` and toasts results. [pages/Documents.jsx](frontend/src/pages/Documents.jsx) consumes `ExtractionSummary` rows (counts inline as `actor_count`/`story_count`/`gap_count`, search switched to `brief_summary`/`brief_tags`); added 4-row skeleton loader and an error card with a Retry button; delete fetches the full record first so undo can re-import via `insertExtraction`. [components/GapsRail.jsx](frontend/src/components/GapsRail.jsx) gap-state actions are now optimistic — write local state, call backend, settle on success or revert with an error toast on failure; mount effect uses an `alive` flag to ignore stale fetches when the user clicks between extractions. **M2.4.2 (react-query) deferred** — current surface (one list, one detail, optimistic gap patches) doesn't need a cache layer; revisit at M2.5/M2.6 when projects + versioning bring cross-page invalidation. Build clean: 57 modules, 249.9KB JS / 5.92KB CSS gzipped to 76.4KB / 2.0KB.
